000471_a610e408-9f38-0478-3726-53182a3b852a
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_a610e408-9f38-0478-3726-53182a3b852a" obligation="normative">
<title id="_b34f00c4-4650-e8b0-01e8-602ad38e0223">Introduction</title>
<p id="_eead8729-5899-9770-4bea-efe007e81a88">The W3C Semantic Web Activity is defining a collection of technologies that enables a “web of data” where information is easily shared and reused across applications. Some key pieces of this technology stack are the RDF (Resource Description Framework) data model <eref type="inline" style="short" bibitemid="RDF" citeas="RDF"/>, <eref type="inline" style="short" bibitemid="RDFS" citeas="RDFS"/>, the OWL Web Ontology Language <eref type="inline" style="short" bibitemid="OWL2" citeas="OWL2"/> and the SPARQL protocol and RDF query language <eref type="inline" style="short" bibitemid="SPARQL" citeas="SPARQL"/>.</p>

<clause id="_a6c8f964-5057-b435-ab0a-baf4449e2e97" obligation="normative">
2



000624_96c8f7cb-aadf-23a7-f990-94502dc21b87
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_96c8f7cb-aadf-23a7-f990-94502dc21b87" obligation="normative">
<title id="_a8eea5cf-44e1-24a5-528c-a94b9fc4fb46">Core</title>
<p id="_83f12ef0-850d-724e-1d3a-448184a522d4" anchor="core">This clause establishes the <strong>Core</strong> requirements class, with IRI <tt>/req/core</tt>, which has a single corresponding conformance class, <strong>Core</strong>, with IRI <tt>/conf/core</tt>. This requirements class defines a set of classes and properties for representing geospatial data. The resulting vocabulary — an ontology — can be used to construct SPARQL graph patterns for querying appropriately modeled geospatial data. The RDFS and OWL vocabularies have both been used so that the vocabulary can be understood by systems that support only RDFS entailment and by systems that support OWL-based reasoning.</p>

<p id="_60bec7eb-e5e8-8c76-264f-12e62a5a9c64">The figure below gives an overview of the classes and properties defined by GeoSPARQL in the <strong>Core</strong>, <strong>Topology Vocabulary Extension</strong> and <strong>Geometry Extension</strong>, <strong>Geometry Topology Extension</strong> and <strong>RDFS Entailment Extension</strong> Conformance Classes.</p>
2



000669_da8abc01-10c6-b03b-1c33-d8e9173790af
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_da8abc01-10c6-b03b-1c33-d8e9173790af" obligation="normative">
<title id="_17953b26-b0a0-b9d5-33aa-9ae3f7808121">Classes</title>
<p id="_eda7841e-372f-76fb-47f0-c8e6cd17be6a">Two main classes are defined: <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>SpatialObject</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:SpatialObject</display-text> </eref> and <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>Feature</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:Feature</display-text> </eref>. The class <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>Feature</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:Feature</display-text> </eref> is equivalent to the UML class <tt>Feature</tt> defined in <xref target="ISO19109" style="short"/>.</p>

<p id="_591d5c5e-d83b-a13d-1cad-ad265c9c1b67">Two container classes are defined: <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>SpatialObjectCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Spatial Object Collection</display-text> </eref> and <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>FeatureCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Feature Collection</display-text> </eref>.</p>

001088_b0445158-0ca4-6409-3f75-1921a700d8f4
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_b0445158-0ca4-6409-3f75-1921a700d8f4" obligation="normative">
<title id="_a74af50e-968e-c0de-381b-b48f53e040c6">Topology Vocabulary Extension</title>
<p id="_3e893029-baa9-21e5-ecfb-53a8e4ec0ac6">This clause establishes the <em>Topology Vocabulary Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class. The IRI base is <tt>/req/topology-vocab-extension</tt>, which has a single corresponding Conformance Class <em>Topology Vocabulary Extension</em>, with IRI <tt>/conf/topology-vocab-extension</tt>. This Requirements class defines a vocabulary for asserting and querying topological relations between spatial objects. The class is parameterized so that different families of topological relations may be used, such as RCC8 and Egenhofer. These relations are generalized so that they may connect features as well as geometries.</p>

<requirement id="_464397ae-0c4d-efa5-5d71-16e004cd244e" model="ogc" type="class" anchor="/req/topology-vocab-extension">
2



001341_fd177836-86b8-282d-8439-df2040c28933
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_fd177836-86b8-282d-8439-df2040c28933" obligation="normative">
<title id="_91dbf936-e362-a02a-0db9-261c080ab2da">Geometry Extension</title>
<p id="_af918c10-f2d3-a70e-9a8d-29e7ad65c7ba">This clause defines the <em>Geometry Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with the base IRI <tt>/req/geometry-extension</tt>. There is a single corresponding conformance class <em>Geometry Extension</em>, with the IRI <tt>/conf/geometry-extension</tt>. These Requirements define a vocabulary for asserting and querying information about geometry data, and define query functions for operating on geometry data.</p>

<requirement id="_61b20c66-43f8-5606-9265-f19b1358fea1" model="ogc" type="class" anchor="/req/geometry-extension">
2

<title id="_ee0b8160-bd15-4d0f-da77-a6406d4f5603">Geometry Class</title>
<p id="_19b3a709-2c0b-1d89-99b1-a96abc77ae3f">A single root geometry class is defined: <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>Geometry</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:Geometry</display-text> </eref>. In addition, properties are defined for describing geometry data and for associating geometries with features.</p>

<p id="_5f77b4ae-c401-685d-0654-fc99f42898b9">One container class is defined: <eref style="short" bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>GeometryCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Geometry Collection</display-text> </eref>.</p>

001738_9db333bb-c34b-d088-a4e0-ea7c565c0fc2
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_9db333bb-c34b-d088-a4e0-ea7c565c0fc2" obligation="normative">
<title id="_a3726b6d-8a66-40b8-2478-67c6bdd56735">Geometry Serializations</title>
<p id="_eaf05417-f01c-28cb-58e4-65b4ceea68c2">This section establishes the Requirements class for representing Geometry data in RDF literals, according to different non-RDF systems.</p>

<p id="_5d4d20f4-788f-e1d3-d252-9245432401d7">GeoSPARQL presents specializations of the <tt>geo:hasSerialization</tt> property for indicating particular serializations and specialized datatype literals for containing them. It does not provide comprehensive definitions of their content since these are given in standards external to GeoSPARQL, all of which are referenced.</p>

002695geometry_​topology_​extension
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_63ccbe4f-e4f9-6759-8147-365c18e88fa6" anchor="geometry_topology_extension" obligation="normative">
<title id="_b36b3ddf-3200-165c-1eae-a7a3f4357c46">Geometry Topology Extension</title>
<p id="_8ca04e1e-cd7a-0324-f1b0-5a200da6d699">This clause establishes the <em>Geometry Topology Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with base IRI <tt>/req/geometry-topology-extension</tt>, which defines a collection of topological query functions that operate on geometry literals. These Requirements are parameterized to give implementations flexibility in the topological relation families and geometry serializations that they choose to support. These Requirements have a single corresponding conformance class <em>Geometry Topology Extension</em>, with IRI <tt>/conf/geometry-topology-extension</tt>.</p>

<p id="_80b21d43-868c-6581-f443-494b44752dd9">The Dimensionally Extended Nine Intersection Model (DE-9IM) <xref target="DE-9IM" style="short"/> has been used to define the relation tested by the query functions introduced in this section. Each query function is associated with a defining DE-9IM intersection pattern. Possible pattern values are:</p>
2
